<pr_description>
[Bug]: Skill short names are exposed but not resolvable by the skill resolver
## Prerequisites
- [x] I will write this issue in English (see the Language Policy)
- [x] I have searched existing issues to avoid duplicates
- [x] I am using the latest version of oh-my-opencode
- [x] I have read the documentation or asked an AI coding agent with this project's GitHub URL loaded and couldn't find the answer

## Bug Description
In an OpenCode environment with oh-my-opencode installed, some superpowers skills are surfaced to the user by their short names (for example `systematic-debugging`), but the `skill` resolver does not actually accept those short names.

Calling the visible short name fails with a `not found` error, and the error message then suggests using the fully qualified name such as `superpowers/systematic-debugging` or the slash-command form `/superpowers:systematic-debugging`.

From a user perspective, this looks like a product bug rather than user error, because the visible skill name is not the same as the executable identifier.

## Steps to Reproduce
1. In the current environment, invoke the skill using the visible short name:
   ```text
   systematic-debugging
   ```
   or call the skill resolver/tool with that same short name.
2. Observe the error:
   ```text
   Skill or command "systematic-debugging" not found. Did you mean: superpowers/systematic-debugging, /superpowers:systematic-debugging?
   ```
3. Retry with the fully qualified name:
   ```text
   superpowers/systematic-debugging
   ```
4. The invocation succeeds.

## Expected Behavior
If a skill is exposed in the available-skills list / UI / context as `systematic-debugging`, that short name should be directly resolvable by the `skill` mechanism.

If short names are intentionally unsupported, then the system should consistently expose only the fully qualified name, so users are not guided toward an invalid invocation.

## Actual Behavior
- The skill is surfaced to the user as a short name like `systematic-debugging`
- The resolver rejects that short name
- The resolver only accepts the fully qualified form such as `superpowers/systematic-debugging`
- The error message teaches the workaround only after the failure happens

## Doctor Output
```shell
$ bunx oh-my-opencode doctor

 oMoMoMoMo Doctor 

 ⚠ 3 issues found:

1. Model override uses unavailable provider
   Provider(s) not found in OpenCode model cache: axonhub, Custom:Nvidia Nim
   Affects: model resolution

2. Comment checker unavailable
   Comment checker binary is not installed.
   Fix: Install @code-yeongyu/comment-checker
   Affects: comment-checker hook

3. Configured models rely on compatibility fallback
   multimodal-looker=google/antigravity-gemini-3-flash (heuristic-backed)
   Affects: multimodal-looker
```

## Error Logs
```shell
Skill or command "systematic-debugging" not found. Did you mean: superpowers/systematic-debugging, /superpowers:systematic-debugging?
```

## Configuration
```json
{
  "note": "No minimal config snippet isolated yet. The issue appears to be in skill name exposure vs resolver namespace handling rather than a user-specific config mistake."
}
```

## Additional Context
My current guess is that the short-name alias is being displayed but not registered in the runtime resolver, or that the resolver is not expanding short names back to the canonical `superpowers/...` identifier.

In other words, the presentation layer and the execution layer seem to disagree about the valid skill identifier.

Current workaround:
- `superpowers/systematic-debugging`
- `/superpowers:systematic-debugging`

## Operating System
macOS

## OpenCode Version
1.3.9

    22	const scopePriority: Record<string, number> = {
    23	  project: 4,
    24	  user: 3,

    58	function mergeNativeSkills(skills: LoadedSkill[], nativeSkills: NativeSkillEntry[]): void {
    59	  const knownNames = new Set(skills.map(skill => skill.name))
    60	  for (const native of nativeSkills) {
    61	    if (knownNames.has(native.name)) continue
    62	    skills.push(nativeSkillToLoadedSkill(native))
    63	    knownNames.add(native.name)
    64	  }
    65	}

    67	function mergeNativeSkillInfos(skillInfos: SkillInfo[], nativeSkills: NativeSkillEntry[]): void {
    68	  const knownNames = new Set(skillInfos.map(skill => skill.name))
    69	  for (const native of nativeSkills) {
    70	    if (knownNames.has(native.name)) continue
    71	    skillInfos.push({
    72	      name: native.name,
    73	      description: native.description,
    74	      location: native.location,
    75	      scope: "config",
    76	    })
    77	    knownNames.add(native.name)
    78	  }
    79	}

    81	function isPromiseLike<T>(value: T | Promise<T>): value is Promise<T> {
    82	  return typeof value === "object" && value !== null && "then" in value
    83	}

    85	function formatCombinedDescription(skills: SkillInfo[], commands: CommandInfo[]): string {
    86	  const lines: string[] = []
    87	
    88	  if (skills.length === 0 && commands.length === 0) {
    89	    return TOOL_DESCRIPTION_NO_SKILLS
    90	  }
    91	
    92	  // Uses module-level scopePriority for consistent priority ordering
    93	
    94	  const allItems: string[] = []
    95	
    96	  // Skills rendered as command items (skills are also slash-invocable)
    97	  if (skills.length > 0) {
    98	    const sortedSkills = [...skills].sort((a, b) => {
    99	      const priorityA = scopePriority[a.scope] || 0
   100	      const priorityB = scopePriority[b.scope] || 0
   101	      return priorityB - priorityA
   102	    })
   103	    sortedSkills.forEach(skill => {
   104	      const parts = [
   105	        "  <command>",
   106	        `    <name>/${skill.name}</name>`,
   107	        `    <description>${skill.description}</description>`,
   108	        `    <scope>${skill.scope}</scope>`,
   109	      ]
   110	      if (skill.compatibility) {
   111	        parts.push(`    <compatibility>${skill.compatibility}</compatibility>`)
   112	      }
   113	      parts.push("  </command>")
   114	      allItems.push(parts.join("\n"))
   115	    })
   116	  }
   117	
   118	  // Sort and add commands second (commands after skills)
   119	  if (commands.length > 0) {
   120	    const sortedCommands = [...commands].sort((a, b) => {
   121	      const priorityA = scopePriority[a.scope] || 0
   122	      const priorityB = scopePriority[b.scope] || 0
   123	      return priorityB - priorityA // Higher priority first
   124	    })
   125	    sortedCommands.forEach(cmd => {
   126	      const hint = cmd.metadata.argumentHint ? ` ${cmd.metadata.argumentHint}` : ""
   127	      const parts = [
   128	        "  <command>",
   129	        `    <name>/${cmd.name}</name>`,
   130	        `    <description>${cmd.metadata.description || "(no description)"}</description>`,
   131	        `    <scope>${cmd.scope}</scope>`,
   132	      ]
   133	      if (hint) {
   134	        parts.push(`    <argument>${hint.trim()}</argument>`)
   135	      }
   136	      parts.push("  </command>")
   137	      allItems.push(parts.join("\n"))
   138	    })
   139	  }
   140	
   141	  if (allItems.length > 0) {
   142	    lines.push(`\n<available_items>\nPriority: project > user > opencode > builtin/plugin | Skills listed before commands\nInvoke via: skill(name="item-name") — omit leading slash for commands.\n${allItems.join("\n")}\n</available_items>`)
   143	  }
   144	
   145	  return TOOL_DESCRIPTION_PREFIX + lines.join("")
   146	}

   148	async function extractSkillBody(skill: LoadedSkill): Promise<string> {
   149	  if (skill.lazyContent) {
   150	    const fullTemplate = await skill.lazyContent.load()
   151	    const templateMatch = fullTemplate.match(/<skill-instruction>([\s\S]*?)<\/skill-instruction>/)
   152	    return templateMatch ? templateMatch[1].trim() : fullTemplate
   153	  }
   154	
   155	  if (skill.scope === "config" && skill.definition.template) {
   156	    const templateMatch = skill.definition.template.match(/<skill-instruction>([\s\S]*?)<\/skill-instruction>/)
   157	    return templateMatch ? templateMatch[1].trim() : skill.definition.template
   158	  }
   159	
   160	  if (skill.path) {
   161	    return extractSkillTemplate(skill)
   162	  }
   163	
   164	  const templateMatch = skill.definition.template?.match(/<skill-instruction>([\s\S]*?)<\/skill-instruction>/)
   165	  return templateMatch ? templateMatch[1].trim() : skill.definition.template || ""
   166	}

   168	async function formatMcpCapabilities(
   169	  skill: LoadedSkill,
   170	  manager: SkillMcpManager,
   171	  sessionID: string
   172	): Promise<string | null> {
   173	  if (!skill.mcpConfig || Object.keys(skill.mcpConfig).length === 0) {
   174	    return null
   175	  }
   176	
   177	  const sections: string[] = ["", "## Available MCP Servers", ""]
   178	
   179	  for (const [serverName, config] of Object.entries(skill.mcpConfig)) {
   180	    const info: SkillMcpClientInfo = {
   181	      serverName,
   182	      skillName: skill.name,
   183	      sessionID,
   184	    }
   185	    const context: SkillMcpServerContext = {
   186	      config,
   187	      skillName: skill.name,
   188	    }
   189	
   190	    sections.push(`### ${serverName}`)
   191	    sections.push("")
   192	
   193	    try {
   194	      const [tools, resources, prompts] = await Promise.all([
   195	        manager.listTools(info, context).catch(() => []),
   196	        manager.listResources(info, context).catch(() => []),
   197	        manager.listPrompts(info, context).catch(() => []),
   198	      ])
   199	
   200	      if (tools.length > 0) {
   201	        sections.push("**Tools:**")
   202	        sections.push("")
   203	        for (const t of tools as Tool[]) {
   204	          sections.push(`#### \`${t.name}\``)
   205	          if (t.description) {
   206	            sections.push(t.description)
   207	          }
   208	          sections.push("")
   209	          sections.push("**inputSchema:**")
   210	          sections.push("```json")
   211	          sections.push(JSON.stringify(sanitizeJsonSchema(t.inputSchema), null, 2))
   212	          sections.push("```")
   213	          sections.push("")
   214	        }
   215	      }
   216	      if (resources.length > 0) {
   217	        sections.push(`**Resources**: ${resources.map((r: Resource) => r.uri).join(", ")}`)
   218	      }
   219	      if (prompts.length > 0) {
   220	        sections.push(`**Prompts**: ${prompts.map((p: Prompt) => p.name).join(", ")}`)
   221	      }
   222	
   223	      if (tools.length === 0 && resources.length === 0 && prompts.length === 0) {
   224	        sections.push("*No capabilities discovered*")
   225	      }
   226	    } catch (error) {
   227	      const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
   228	      sections.push(`*Failed to connect: ${errorMessage.split("\n")[0]}*`)
   229	    }
   230	
   231	    sections.push("")
   232	    sections.push(`Use \`skill_mcp\` tool with \`mcp_name="${serverName}"\` to invoke.`)
   233	    sections.push("")
   234	  }
   235	
   236	  return sections.join("\n")
   237	}

   239	export function createSkillTool(options: SkillLoadOptions = {}): ToolDefinition {
   240	  let cachedDescription: string | null = null
   241	
   242	  const getSkills = async (): Promise<LoadedSkill[]> => {
   243	    clearSkillCache()
   244	    const discovered = await getAllSkills({disabledSkills: options?.disabledSkills, browserProvider: options?.browserProvider})
   245	    const allSkills = !options.skills
   246	      ? discovered
   247	      : [...discovered, ...options.skills.filter(s => !new Set(discovered.map(d => d.name)).has(s.name))]
   248	
   249	    if (options.nativeSkills) {
   250	      try {
   251	        const nativeAll = await options.nativeSkills.all()
   252	        mergeNativeSkills(allSkills, nativeAll)
   253	      } catch {
   254	        // Native skill discovery may not be available
   255	      }
   256	    }
   257	
   258	    return allSkills
   259	  }
   260	
   261	  const getCommands = (): CommandInfo[] => {
   262	    return discoverCommandsSync(undefined, {
   263	      pluginsEnabled: options.pluginsEnabled,
   264	      enabledPluginsOverride: options.enabledPluginsOverride,
   265	    })
   266	  }
   267	
   268	  const buildDescription = async (force = false): Promise<string> => {
   269	    if (!force && cachedDescription) return cachedDescription
   270	    const skills = await getSkills()
   271	    const commands = getCommands()
   272	    const skillInfos = skills.map(loadedSkillToInfo)
   273	    cachedDescription = formatCombinedDescription(skillInfos, commands)
   274	    return cachedDescription
   275	  }
   276	
   277	  if (options.skills !== undefined) {
   278	    const skillInfos = options.skills.map(loadedSkillToInfo)
   279	    const commandsForDescription = options.commands ?? []
   280	    let needsAsyncRefresh = false
   281	
   282	    if (options.nativeSkills) {
   283	      try {
   284	        const nativeAll = options.nativeSkills.all()
   285	        if (isPromiseLike(nativeAll)) {
   286	          needsAsyncRefresh = true
   287	        } else {
   288	          mergeNativeSkillInfos(skillInfos, nativeAll)
   289	        }
   290	      } catch {
   291	        // Native skill discovery may not be available
   292	      }
   293	    }
   294	
   295	    cachedDescription = formatCombinedDescription(skillInfos, commandsForDescription)
   296	    if (needsAsyncRefresh) {
   297	      void buildDescription(true)
   298	    }
   299	  } else if (options.commands !== undefined) {
   300	    cachedDescription = formatCombinedDescription([], options.commands)
   301	  } else {
   302	    void buildDescription()
   303	  }
   304	
   305	  return tool({
   306	    get description() {
   307	      if (cachedDescription === null) {
   308	        void buildDescription()
   309	      }
   310	      return cachedDescription ?? TOOL_DESCRIPTION_PREFIX
   311	    },
   312	    args: {
   313	      name: tool.schema.string().describe("The skill or command name (e.g., 'code-review' or 'publish'). Use without leading slash for commands."),
   314	      user_message: tool.schema
   315	        .string()
   316	        .optional()
   317	        .describe("Optional arguments or context for command invocation. Example: name='publish', user_message='patch'"),
   318	    },
   319	    async execute(args: SkillArgs, ctx?: { agent?: string }) {
   320	      const skills = await getSkills()
   321	      const commands = getCommands()
   322	      cachedDescription = formatCombinedDescription(skills.map(loadedSkillToInfo), commands)
   323	
   324	      const requestedName = args.name.replace(/^\//, "")
   325	
   326	      // Check skills first (exact match, case-insensitive)
   327	      const matchedSkill = skills.find(s => s.name.toLowerCase() === requestedName.toLowerCase())
   328	
   329	      if (matchedSkill) {
   330	        if (matchedSkill.definition.agent && (!ctx?.agent || matchedSkill.definition.agent !== ctx.agent)) {
   331	          throw new Error(`Skill "${matchedSkill.name}" is restricted to agent "${matchedSkill.definition.agent}"`)
   332	        }
   333	
   334	        let body = await extractSkillBody(matchedSkill)
   335	
   336	        if (matchedSkill.name === "git-master") {
   337	          body = injectGitMasterConfig(body, options.gitMasterConfig)
   338	        }
   339	
   340	        const dir = matchedSkill.path ? dirname(matchedSkill.path) : matchedSkill.resolvedPath || process.cwd()
   341	
   342	        const output = [
   343	          `## Skill: ${matchedSkill.name}`,
   344	          "",
   345	          `**Base directory**: ${dir}`,
   346	          "",
   347	          body,
   348	        ]
   349	
   350	        if (options.mcpManager && options.getSessionID && matchedSkill.mcpConfig) {
   351	          const mcpInfo = await formatMcpCapabilities(
   352	            matchedSkill,
   353	            options.mcpManager,
   354	            options.getSessionID()
   355	          )
   356	          if (mcpInfo) {
   357	            output.push(mcpInfo)
   358	          }
   359	        }
   360	
   361	        return output.join("\n")
   362	      }
   363	
   364	      // Check commands (exact match, case-insensitive) - sort by priority first
   365	      const sortedCommands = [...commands].sort((a, b) => {
   366	        const priorityA = scopePriority[a.scope] || 0
   367	        const priorityB = scopePriority[b.scope] || 0
   368	        return priorityB - priorityA // Higher priority first
   369	      })
   370	      const matchedCommand = sortedCommands.find(c => c.name.toLowerCase() === requestedName.toLowerCase())
   371	
   372	      if (matchedCommand) {
   373	        return await formatLoadedCommand(matchedCommand, args.user_message)
   374	      }
   375	
   376	      // No match found — provide helpful error with partial matches
   377	      const allNames = [
   378	        ...skills.map(s => s.name),
   379	        ...commands.map(c => `/${c.name}`),
   380	      ]
   381	
   382	      const partialMatches = allNames.filter(n =>
   383	        n.toLowerCase().includes(requestedName.toLowerCase())
   384	      )
   385	
   386	      if (partialMatches.length > 0) {
   387	        throw new Error(
   388	          `Skill or command "${args.name}" not found. Did you mean: ${partialMatches.join(", ")}?`
   389	        )
   390	      }
   391	
   392	      const available = allNames.join(", ")
   393	      throw new Error(
   394	        `Skill or command "${args.name}" not found. Available: ${available || "none"}`
   395	      )
   396	    },
   397	  })
   398	}
   399	
   400	export const skill: ToolDefinition = createSkillTool()
   401

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/src/features/opencode-skill-loader/skill-discovery.ts:
     1	import { createBuiltinSkills } from "../builtin-skills/skills"
     2	import { discoverSkills } from "./loader"
     3	import type { LoadedSkill } from "./types"
     4	import type { SkillResolutionOptions } from "./skill-resolution-options"
     5	
     6	const cachedSkillsByProvider = new Map<string, LoadedSkill[]>()
     7	
     8	export function clearSkillCache(): void {
     9	        cachedSkillsByProvider.clear()
    10	}
    11	
    12	export async function getAllSkills(options?: SkillResolutionOptions): Promise<LoadedSkill[]> {
    13	        const cacheKey = options?.browserProvider ?? "playwright"
    14	        const hasDisabledSkills = options?.disabledSkills && options.disabledSkills.size > 0
    15	
    16	        // Skip cache if disabledSkills is provided (varies between calls)
    17	        if (!hasDisabledSkills) {
    18	                const cached = cachedSkillsByProvider.get(cacheKey)
    19	                if (cached) return cached
    20	        }
    21	
    22	        const [discoveredSkills, builtinSkillDefinitions] = await Promise.all([
    23	                discoverSkills({ includeClaudeCodePaths: true, directory: options?.directory }),
    24	                Promise.resolve(
    25	                        createBuiltinSkills({
    26	                                browserProvider: options?.browserProvider,
    27	                                disabledSkills: options?.disabledSkills,
    28	                        })
    29	                ),
    30	        ])
    31	
    32	        const builtinSkillsAsLoaded: LoadedSkill[] = builtinSkillDefinitions.map((skill) => ({
    33	                name: skill.name,
    34	                definition: {
    35	                        name: skill.name,
    36	                        description: skill.description,
    37	                        template: skill.template,
    38	                        model: skill.model,
    39	                        agent: skill.agent,
    40	                        subtask: skill.subtask,
    41	                },
    42	                scope: "builtin" as const,
    43	                license: skill.license,
    44	                compatibility: skill.compatibility,
    45	                metadata: skill.metadata as Record<string, string> | undefined,
    46	                allowedTools: skill.allowedTools,
    47	                mcpConfig: skill.mcpConfig,
    48	        }))
    49	
    50	        // Provider-gated skill names that should be filtered based on browserProvider
    51	        const providerGatedSkillNames = new Set(["agent-browser", "playwright"])
    52	        const browserProvider = options?.browserProvider ?? "playwright"
    53	
    54	        // Filter discovered skills to exclude provider-gated names that don't match the selected provider
    55	        const filteredDiscoveredSkills = discoveredSkills.filter((skill) => {
    56	                if (!providerGatedSkillNames.has(skill.name)) {
    57	                        return true
    58	                }
    59	                // For provider-gated skills, only include if it matches the selected provider
    60	                return skill.name === browserProvider
    61	        })
    62	
    63	        const discoveredNames = new Set(filteredDiscoveredSkills.map((skill) => skill.name))
    64	        const uniqueBuiltins = builtinSkillsAsLoaded.filter((skill) => !discoveredNames.has(skill.name))
    65	
    66	        let allSkills = [...filteredDiscoveredSkills, ...uniqueBuiltins]
    67	
    68	        // Filter discovered skills by disabledSkills (builtin skills are already filtered by createBuiltinSkills)
    69	        if (hasDisabledSkills) {
    70	                allSkills = allSkills.filter((skill) => !options!.disabledSkills!.has(skill.name))
    71	        } else {
    72	                cachedSkillsByProvider.set(cacheKey, allSkills)
    73	        }
    74	
    75	        return allSkills
    76	}
    77

     1	import type { BuiltinSkill } from "./types"
     2	import type { BrowserAutomationProvider } from "../../config/schema"
     3	
     4	import {
     5	  playwrightSkill,
     6	  agentBrowserSkill,
     7	  playwrightCliSkill,
     8	  frontendUiUxSkill,
     9	  gitMasterSkill,
    10	  devBrowserSkill,
    11	  reviewWorkSkill,
    12	  aiSlopRemoverSkill,
    13	} from "./skills/index"
    14	
    15	export interface CreateBuiltinSkillsOptions {
    16	  browserProvider?: BrowserAutomationProvider
    17	  disabledSkills?: Set<string>
    18	}
    19	
    20	export function createBuiltinSkills(options: CreateBuiltinSkillsOptions = {}): BuiltinSkill[] {
    21	  const { browserProvider = "playwright", disabledSkills } = options
    22	
    23	  let browserSkill: BuiltinSkill
    24	  if (browserProvider === "agent-browser") {
    25	    browserSkill = agentBrowserSkill
    26	  } else if (browserProvider === "playwright-cli") {
    27	    browserSkill = playwrightCliSkill
    28	  } else {
    29	    browserSkill = playwrightSkill
    30	  }
    31	
    32	  const skills = [browserSkill, frontendUiUxSkill, gitMasterSkill, devBrowserSkill, reviewWorkSkill, aiSlopRemoverSkill]
    33	
    34	  if (!disabledSkills) {
    35	    return skills
    36	  }
    37	
    38	  return skills.filter((skill) => !disabledSkills.has(skill.name))
    39	}

   391	      createMockSkillWithScope("project-skill", "project"),

   401	    //#then: skills should appear as <command> items with / prefix, listed before regular commands

   406	    const skillCmdIndex = desc.indexOf("/project-skill")

     1	import { promises as fs } from "fs"
     2	import { join } from "path"
     3	import { resolveSymlinkAsync, isMarkdownFile } from "../../shared/file-utils"
     4	import type { LoadedSkill, SkillScope } from "./types"
     5	import { inferSkillNameFromFileName, loadSkillFromPath } from "./loaded-skill-from-path"
     6	
     7	export async function loadSkillsFromDir(options: {
     8	  skillsDir: string
     9	  scope: SkillScope
    10	  namePrefix?: string
    11	  depth?: number
    12	  maxDepth?: number
    13	}): Promise<LoadedSkill[]> {
    14	  const namePrefix = options.namePrefix ?? ""
    15	  const depth = options.depth ?? 0
    16	  const maxDepth = options.maxDepth ?? 2
    17	
    18	  const entries = await fs.readdir(options.skillsDir, { withFileTypes: true }).catch(() => [])
    19	  const skillMap = new Map<string, LoadedSkill>()
    20	
    21	  const directories = entries.filter(
    22	    (entry) => !entry.name.startsWith(".") && (entry.isDirectory() || entry.isSymbolicLink())
    23	  )
    24	  const files = entries.filter(
    25	    (entry) =>
    26	      !entry.name.startsWith(".") &&
    27	      !entry.isDirectory() &&
    28	      !entry.isSymbolicLink() &&
    29	      isMarkdownFile(entry)
    30	  )
    31	
    32	  for (const entry of directories) {
    33	    const entryPath = join(options.skillsDir, entry.name)
    34	    const resolvedPath = await resolveSymlinkAsync(entryPath)
    35	    const dirName = entry.name
    36	
    37	    const skillMdPath = join(resolvedPath, "SKILL.md")
    38	    try {
    39	      await fs.access(skillMdPath)
    40	      const skill = await loadSkillFromPath({
    41	        skillPath: skillMdPath,
    42	        resolvedPath,
    43	        defaultName: dirName,
    44	        scope: options.scope,
    45	        namePrefix,
    46	      })
    47	      if (skill && !skillMap.has(skill.name)) {
    48	        skillMap.set(skill.name, skill)
    49	      }
    50	      continue
    51	    } catch {
    52	      // no SKILL.md
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    const namedSkillMdPath = join(resolvedPath, `${dirName}.md`)
    56	    try {
    57	      await fs.access(namedSkillMdPath)
    58	      const skill = await loadSkillFromPath({
    59	        skillPath: namedSkillMdPath,
    60	        resolvedPath,
    61	        defaultName: dirName,
    62	        scope: options.scope,
    63	        namePrefix,
    64	      })
    65	      if (skill && !skillMap.has(skill.name)) {
    66	        skillMap.set(skill.name, skill)
    67	      }
    68	      continue
    69	    } catch {
    70	      // no named md
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    if (depth < maxDepth) {
    74	      const newPrefix = namePrefix ? `${namePrefix}/${dirName}` : dirName
    75	      const nestedSkills = await loadSkillsFromDir({
    76	        skillsDir: resolvedPath,
    77	        scope: options.scope,
    78	        namePrefix: newPrefix,
    79	        depth: depth + 1,
    80	        maxDepth,
    81	      })
    82	      for (const nestedSkill of nestedSkills) {
    83	        if (!skillMap.has(nestedSkill.name)) {
    84	          skillMap.set(nestedSkill.name, nestedSkill)
    85	        }
    86	      }
    87	    }
    88	  }
    89	
    90	  for (const entry of files) {
    91	    const entryPath = join(options.skillsDir, entry.name)
    92	    const baseName = inferSkillNameFromFileName(entryPath)
    93	    const skill = await loadSkillFromPath({
    94	      skillPath: entryPath,
    95	      resolvedPath: options.skillsDir,
    96	      defaultName: baseName,
    97	      scope: options.scope,
    98	      namePrefix,
    99	    })
   100	    if (skill && !skillMap.has(skill.name)) {
   101	      skillMap.set(skill.name, skill)
   102	    }
   103	  }
   104	
   105	  return Array.from(skillMap.values())
   106	}
   107

     1	import { promises as fs } from "fs"
     2	import { basename } from "path"
     3	import { parseFrontmatter } from "../../shared/frontmatter"
     4	import { sanitizeModelField } from "../../shared/model-sanitizer"
     5	import { resolveSkillPathReferences } from "../../shared/skill-path-resolver"
     6	import type { CommandDefinition } from "../claude-code-command-loader/types"
     7	import { parseAllowedTools } from "./allowed-tools-parser"
     8	import { loadMcpJsonFromDir, parseSkillMcpConfigFromFrontmatter } from "./skill-mcp-config"
     9	import type { SkillScope, SkillMetadata, LoadedSkill, LazyContentLoader } from "./types"
    10	
    11	export async function loadSkillFromPath(options: {
    12	  skillPath: string
    13	  resolvedPath: string
    14	  defaultName: string
    15	  scope: SkillScope
    16	  namePrefix?: string
    17	}): Promise<LoadedSkill | null> {
    18	  const namePrefix = options.namePrefix ?? ""
    19	
    20	  try {
    21	    const content = await fs.readFile(options.skillPath, "utf-8")
    22	    const { data, body } = parseFrontmatter<SkillMetadata>(content)
    23	
    24	    const frontmatterMcp = parseSkillMcpConfigFromFrontmatter(content)
    25	    const mcpJsonMcp = await loadMcpJsonFromDir(options.resolvedPath)
    26	    const mcpConfig = mcpJsonMcp || frontmatterMcp
    27	
    28	    const baseName = data.name || options.defaultName
    29	    const skillName = namePrefix ? `${namePrefix}/${baseName}` : baseName
    30	    const originalDescription = data.description || ""
    31	    const isOpencodeSource = options.scope === "opencode" || options.scope === "opencode-project"
    32	    const formattedDescription = `(${options.scope} - Skill) ${originalDescription}`
    33	
    34	    const resolvedBody = resolveSkillPathReferences(body.trim(), options.resolvedPath)
    35	    const templateContent = `<skill-instruction>\nBase directory for this skill: ${options.resolvedPath}/\nFile references (@path) in this skill are relative to this directory.\n\n${resolvedBody}\n</skill-instruction>\n\n<user-request>\n$ARGUMENTS\n</user-request>`
    36	
    37	    const eagerLoader: LazyContentLoader = {
    38	      loaded: true,
    39	      content: templateContent,
    40	      load: async () => templateContent,
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    const definition: CommandDefinition = {
    44	      name: skillName,
    45	      description: formattedDescription,
    46	      template: templateContent,
    47	      model: sanitizeModelField(data.model, isOpencodeSource ? "opencode" : "claude-code"),
    48	      agent: data.agent,
    49	      subtask: data.subtask,
    50	      argumentHint: data["argument-hint"],
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    return {
    54	      name: skillName,
    55	      path: options.skillPath,
    56	      resolvedPath: options.resolvedPath,
    57	      definition,
    58	      scope: options.scope,
    59	      license: data.license,
    60	      compatibility: data.compatibility,
    61	      metadata: data.metadata,
    62	      allowedTools: parseAllowedTools(data["allowed-tools"]),
    63	      mcpConfig,
    64	      lazyContent: eagerLoader,
    65	    }
    66	  } catch {
    67	    return null
    68	  }
    69	}
    70	
    71	export function inferSkillNameFromFileName(filePath: string): string {
    72	  return basename(filePath, ".md")
    73	}

     1	import type { AvailableSkill } from "../agents/dynamic-agent-prompt-builder"
     2	import type { OhMyOpenCodeConfig } from "../config"
     3	import type { BrowserAutomationProvider } from "../config/schema/browser-automation"
     4	import type {
     5	  LoadedSkill,
     6	  SkillScope,
     7	} from "../features/opencode-skill-loader/types"
     8	
     9	import {
    10	  discoverConfigSourceSkills,
    11	  discoverUserClaudeSkills,
    12	  discoverProjectClaudeSkills,
    13	  discoverOpencodeGlobalSkills,
    14	  discoverOpencodeProjectSkills,
    15	  discoverProjectAgentsSkills,
    16	  discoverGlobalAgentsSkills,
    17	  mergeSkills,
    18	} from "../features/opencode-skill-loader"
    19	import { createBuiltinSkills } from "../features/builtin-skills"
    20	import { getSystemMcpServerNames } from "../features/claude-code-mcp-loader"
    21	
    22	export type SkillContext = {
    23	  mergedSkills: LoadedSkill[]
    24	  availableSkills: AvailableSkill[]
    25	  browserProvider: BrowserAutomationProvider
    26	  disabledSkills: Set<string>
    27	}
    28	
    29	const PROVIDER_GATED_SKILL_NAMES = new Set(["agent-browser", "playwright"])
    30	
    31	function mapScopeToLocation(scope: SkillScope): AvailableSkill["location"] {
    32	  if (scope === "user" || scope === "opencode") return "user"
    33	  if (scope === "project" || scope === "opencode-project") return "project"
    34	  return "plugin"
    35	}
    36	
    37	function filterProviderGatedSkills(
    38	  skills: LoadedSkill[],
    39	  browserProvider: BrowserAutomationProvider,
    40	): LoadedSkill[] {
    41	  return skills.filter((skill) => {
    42	    if (!PROVIDER_GATED_SKILL_NAMES.has(skill.name)) {
    43	      return true
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    return skill.name === browserProvider
    47	  })
    48	}
    49	
    50	export async function createSkillContext(args: {
    51	  directory: string
    52	  pluginConfig: OhMyOpenCodeConfig
    53	}): Promise<SkillContext> {
    54	  const { directory, pluginConfig } = args
    55	
    56	  const browserProvider: BrowserAutomationProvider =
    57	    pluginConfig.browser_automation_engine?.provider ?? "playwright"
    58	
    59	  const disabledSkills = new Set<string>(pluginConfig.disabled_skills ?? [])
    60	  const systemMcpNames = getSystemMcpServerNames()
    61	
    62	  const builtinSkills = createBuiltinSkills({
    63	    browserProvider,
    64	    disabledSkills,
    65	  }).filter((skill) => {
    66	    if (skill.mcpConfig) {
    67	      for (const mcpName of Object.keys(skill.mcpConfig)) {
    68	        if (systemMcpNames.has(mcpName)) return false
    69	      }
    70	    }
    71	    return true
    72	  })
    73	
    74	  const includeClaudeSkills = pluginConfig.claude_code?.skills !== false
    75	  const [configSourceSkills, userSkills, globalSkills, projectSkills, opencodeProjectSkills, agentsProjectSkills, agentsGlobalSkills] =
    76	    await Promise.all([
    77	      discoverConfigSourceSkills({
    78	        config: pluginConfig.skills,
    79	        configDir: directory,
    80	      }),
    81	      includeClaudeSkills ? discoverUserClaudeSkills() : Promise.resolve([]),
    82	      discoverOpencodeGlobalSkills(),
    83	      includeClaudeSkills ? discoverProjectClaudeSkills(directory) : Promise.resolve([]),
    84	      discoverOpencodeProjectSkills(directory),
    85	      discoverProjectAgentsSkills(directory),
    86	      discoverGlobalAgentsSkills(),
    87	    ])
    88	
    89	  const filteredConfigSourceSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(
    90	    configSourceSkills,
    91	    browserProvider,
    92	  )
    93	  const filteredUserSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(userSkills, browserProvider)
    94	  const filteredGlobalSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(globalSkills, browserProvider)
    95	  const filteredProjectSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(projectSkills, browserProvider)
    96	  const filteredOpencodeProjectSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(
    97	    opencodeProjectSkills,
    98	    browserProvider,
    99	  )
   100	  const filteredAgentsProjectSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(
   101	    agentsProjectSkills,
   102	    browserProvider,
   103	  )
   104	  const filteredAgentsGlobalSkills = filterProviderGatedSkills(
   105	    agentsGlobalSkills,
   106	    browserProvider,
   107	  )
   108	
   109	  const mergedSkills = mergeSkills(
   110	    builtinSkills,
   111	    pluginConfig.skills,
   112	    filteredConfigSourceSkills,
   113	    [...filteredUserSkills, ...filteredAgentsGlobalSkills],
   114	    filteredGlobalSkills,
   115	    [...filteredProjectSkills, ...filteredAgentsProjectSkills],
   116	    filteredOpencodeProjectSkills,
   117	    { configDir: directory },
   118	  )
   119	
   120	  const availableSkills: AvailableSkill[] = mergedSkills.map((skill) => ({
   121	    name: skill.name,
   122	    description: skill.definition.description ?? "",
   123	    location: mapScopeToLocation(skill.scope),
   124	  }))
   125	
   126	  return {
   127	    mergedSkills,
   128	    availableSkills,
   129	    browserProvider,
   130	    disabledSkills,
   131	  }
   132	}
   133

     1	import type { LoadedSkill } from "./types"
     2	import type { SkillsConfig } from "../../config/schema"
     3	import type { BuiltinSkill } from "../builtin-skills/types"
     4	import { builtinToLoadedSkill } from "./merger/builtin-skill-converter"
     5	import { configEntryToLoadedSkill } from "./merger/config-skill-entry-loader"
     6	import { mergeSkillDefinitions } from "./merger/skill-definition-merger"
     7	import { normalizeSkillsConfig } from "./merger/skills-config-normalizer"
     8	import { SCOPE_PRIORITY } from "./merger/scope-priority"
     9	
    10	export interface MergeSkillsOptions {
    11	  configDir?: string
    12	}
    13	
    14	export function mergeSkills(
    15	  builtinSkills: BuiltinSkill[],
    16	  config: SkillsConfig | undefined,
    17	  configSourceSkills: LoadedSkill[],
    18	  userClaudeSkills: LoadedSkill[],
    19	  userOpencodeSkills: LoadedSkill[],
    20	  projectClaudeSkills: LoadedSkill[],
    21	  projectOpencodeSkills: LoadedSkill[],
    22	  options: MergeSkillsOptions = {}
    23	): LoadedSkill[] {
    24	  const skillMap = new Map<string, LoadedSkill>()
    25	
    26	  for (const builtin of builtinSkills) {
    27	    const loaded = builtinToLoadedSkill(builtin)
    28	    skillMap.set(loaded.name, loaded)
    29	  }
    30	
    31	  const normalizedConfig = normalizeSkillsConfig(config)
    32	
    33	  for (const [name, entry] of Object.entries(normalizedConfig.entries)) {
    34	    if (entry === false) continue
    35	    if (entry === true) continue
    36	
    37	    if (entry.disable) continue
    38	
    39	    const loaded = configEntryToLoadedSkill(name, entry, options.configDir)
    40	    if (loaded) {
    41	      const existing = skillMap.get(name)
    42	      if (existing && !entry.template && !entry.from) {
    43	        skillMap.set(name, mergeSkillDefinitions(existing, entry))
    44	      } else {
    45	        skillMap.set(name, loaded)
    46	      }
    47	    }
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  const fileSystemSkills = [
    51	    ...configSourceSkills,
    52	    ...userClaudeSkills,
    53	    ...userOpencodeSkills,
    54	    ...projectClaudeSkills,
    55	    ...projectOpencodeSkills,
    56	  ]
    57	
    58	  for (const skill of fileSystemSkills) {
    59	    const existing = skillMap.get(skill.name)
    60	    if (!existing || SCOPE_PRIORITY[skill.scope] > SCOPE_PRIORITY[existing.scope]) {
    61	      skillMap.set(skill.name, skill)
    62	    }
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  for (const [name, entry] of Object.entries(normalizedConfig.entries)) {
    66	    if (entry === true) continue
    67	    if (entry === false) {
    68	      skillMap.delete(name)
    69	      continue
    70	    }
    71	    if (entry.disable) {
    72	      skillMap.delete(name)
    73	      continue
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    const existing = skillMap.get(name)
    77	    if (existing && !entry.template && !entry.from) {
    78	      skillMap.set(name, mergeSkillDefinitions(existing, entry))
    79	    }
    80	  }
    81	
    82	  for (const name of normalizedConfig.disable) {
    83	    skillMap.delete(name)
    84	  }
    85	
    86	  if (normalizedConfig.enable.length > 0) {
    87	    const enableSet = new Set(normalizedConfig.enable)
    88	    for (const name of skillMap.keys()) {
    89	      if (!enableSet.has(name)) {
    90	        skillMap.delete(name)
    91	      }
    92	    }
    93	  }
    94	
    95	  return Array.from(skillMap.values())
    96	}

    12	export type CreateToolsResult = {

    14	  mergedSkills: LoadedSkill[]

    44	  "session_list",
    45	  "session_read",
    46	  "session_search",

    48	  "interactive_bash",
    49	  "look_at",

    73	export function trimToolsToCap(filteredTools: ToolsRecord, maxTools: number): void {
    74	  const toolNames = Object.keys(filteredTools)
    75	  if (toolNames.length <= maxTools) return
    76	
    77	  const removableToolNames = [
    78	    ...LOW_PRIORITY_TOOL_ORDER.filter((toolName) => toolNames.includes(toolName)),
    79	    ...toolNames
    80	      .filter((toolName) => !LOW_PRIORITY_TOOL_ORDER.includes(toolName as (typeof LOW_PRIORITY_TOOL_ORDER)[number]))
    81	      .sort(),
    82	  ]
    83	
    84	  let currentCount = toolNames.length
    85	  let removed = 0
    86	
    87	  for (const toolName of removableToolNames) {
    88	    if (currentCount <= maxTools) break
    89	    if (!filteredTools[toolName]) continue
    90	    delete filteredTools[toolName]
    91	    currentCount -= 1
    92	    removed += 1
    93	  }
    94	
    95	  log(
    96	    `[tool-registry] Trimmed ${removed} tools to satisfy max_tools=${maxTools}. Final plugin tool count=${currentCount}.`,
    97	  )
    98	}

   100	export function createToolRegistry(args: {
   101	  ctx: PluginContext

   120	  )

   135	    sisyphusAgentConfig: pluginConfig.sisyphus_agent,
   136	    syncPollTimeoutMs: pluginConfig.background_task?.syncPollTimeoutMs,
   137	    onSyncSessionCreated: async (event) => {
   138	      log("[index] onSyncSessionCreated callback", {
   139	        sessionID: event.sessionID,

   151	        },

   153	    },
   154	  })
   155

   157

   161	    getSessionID: getSessionIDForMcp,
   162	  })

   166	    enabledPluginsOverride: pluginConfig.claude_code?.plugins_override,
   167	  })

   171	    mcpManager: managers.skillMcpManager,
   172	    getSessionID: getSessionIDForMcp,
   173	    gitMasterConfig: pluginConfig.git_master,
   174	    browserProvider: skillContext.browserProvider,
   175	    nativeSkills: "skills" in ctx ? (ctx as { skills: SkillLoadOptions["nativeSkills"] }).skills : undefined,
   176	  })
   177	
   178	  // task_system defaults to true since v3.14 — delegation (oracle, subagents) requires it
   179	  const taskSystemEnabled = pluginConfig.experimental?.task_system ?? true
   180	  const taskToolsRecord: Record<string, ToolDefinition> = taskSystemEnabled
   181	    ? {
   182	        task_create: createTaskCreateTool(pluginConfig, ctx),
   183	        task_get: createTaskGetTool(pluginConfig),
   184	        task_list: createTaskList(pluginConfig),

   186	      }
   187	    : {}
   188	
   189	  const hashlineEnabled = pluginConfig.hashline_edit ?? false

   191	    ? { edit: createHashlineEditTool(ctx) }
   192	    : {}
   193

   206	    interactive_bash,
   207	    ...taskToolsRecord,
   208	    ...hashlineToolsRecord,
   209	  }
   210	
   211	  for (const toolDefinition of Object.values(allTools)) {
   212	    normalizeToolArgSchemas(toolDefinition)
   213	  }
   214	
   215	  const filteredTools: ToolsRecord = filterDisabledTools(allTools, pluginConfig.disabled_tools)
   216	
   217	  const maxTools = pluginConfig.experimental?.max_tools

   220	  }
   221

   223	    filteredTools,
   224	    taskSystemEnabled,
   225	  }
   226	}

     1	import { promises as fs } from "fs"
     2	import { homedir } from "os"
     3	import { dirname, extname, isAbsolute, join, relative } from "path"
     4	import picomatch from "picomatch"
     5	import type { SkillsConfig } from "../../config/schema"
     6	import { normalizeSkillsConfig } from "./merger/skills-config-normalizer"
     7	import { deduplicateSkillsByName } from "./skill-deduplication"
     8	import { loadSkillsFromDir } from "./skill-directory-loader"
     9	import { inferSkillNameFromFileName, loadSkillFromPath } from "./loaded-skill-from-path"
    10	import type { LoadedSkill } from "./types"
    11	
    12	const MAX_RECURSIVE_DEPTH = 10
    13	
    14	function isHttpUrl(path: string): boolean {
    15	  return path.startsWith("http://") || path.startsWith("https://")
    16	}
    17	
    18	function toAbsolutePath(path: string, configDir: string): string {
    19	  if (path === "~") {
    20	    return homedir()
    21	  }
    22	
    23	  if (path.startsWith("~/")) {
    24	    return join(homedir(), path.slice(2))
    25	  }
    26	
    27	  if (isAbsolute(path)) {
    28	    return path
    29	  }
    30	  return join(configDir, path)
    31	}
    32	
    33	function isMarkdownPath(path: string): boolean {
    34	  return extname(path).toLowerCase() === ".md"
    35	}
    36	
    37	export function normalizePathForGlob(path: string): string {
    38	  return path.split("\\").join("/")
    39	}
    40	
    41	function filterByGlob(skills: LoadedSkill[], sourceBaseDir: string, globPattern?: string): LoadedSkill[] {
    42	  if (!globPattern) return skills
    43	
    44	  return skills.filter((skill) => {
    45	    if (!skill.path) return false
    46	    const rel = normalizePathForGlob(relative(sourceBaseDir, skill.path))
    47	    return picomatch.isMatch(rel, globPattern, { dot: true, bash: true })
    48	  })
    49	}
    50	
    51	async function loadSourcePath(options: {
    52	  sourcePath: string
    53	  recursive: boolean
    54	  globPattern?: string
    55	  configDir: string
    56	}): Promise<LoadedSkill[]> {
    57	  if (isHttpUrl(options.sourcePath)) {
    58	    return []
    59	  }
    60	
    61	  const absolutePath = toAbsolutePath(options.sourcePath, options.configDir)
    62	  const stat = await fs.stat(absolutePath).catch(() => null)
    63	  if (!stat) return []
    64	
    65	  if (stat.isFile()) {
    66	    if (!isMarkdownPath(absolutePath)) return []
    67	    const loaded = await loadSkillFromPath({
    68	      skillPath: absolutePath,
    69	      resolvedPath: dirname(absolutePath),
    70	      defaultName: inferSkillNameFromFileName(absolutePath),
    71	      scope: "config",
    72	    })
    73	    if (!loaded) return []
    74	    return filterByGlob([loaded], dirname(absolutePath), options.globPattern)
    75	  }
    76	
    77	  if (!stat.isDirectory()) return []
    78	
    79	  const directorySkills = await loadSkillsFromDir({
    80	    skillsDir: absolutePath,
    81	    scope: "config",
    82	    maxDepth: options.recursive ? MAX_RECURSIVE_DEPTH : 0,
    83	  })
    84	  return filterByGlob(directorySkills, absolutePath, options.globPattern)
    85	}
    86	
    87	export async function discoverConfigSourceSkills(options: {
    88	  config: SkillsConfig | undefined
    89	  configDir: string
    90	}): Promise<LoadedSkill[]> {
    91	  const normalized = normalizeSkillsConfig(options.config)
    92	  if (normalized.sources.length === 0) return []
    93	
    94	  const loadedBySource = await Promise.all(
    95	    normalized.sources.map((source) => {
    96	      if (typeof source === "string") {
    97	        return loadSourcePath({
    98	          sourcePath: source,
    99	          recursive: false,
   100	          configDir: options.configDir,
   101	        })
   102	      }
   103	
   104	      return loadSourcePath({
   105	        sourcePath: source.path,
   106	        recursive: source.recursive ?? false,
   107	        globPattern: source.glob,
   108	        configDir: options.configDir,
   109	      })
   110	    }),
   111	  )
   112	
   113	  return deduplicateSkillsByName(loadedBySource.flat())
   114	}

     1	import { isAbsolute, relative, resolve, sep } from "node:path"
     2	
     3	function looksLikeFilePath(path: string): boolean {
     4	        if (path.endsWith("/")) return true
     5	        const lastSegment = path.split("/").pop() ?? ""
     6	        return /\.[a-zA-Z0-9]+$/.test(lastSegment)
     7	}
     8	
     9	export function resolveSkillPathReferences(content: string, basePath: string): string {
    10	        const normalizedBase = basePath.endsWith("/") ? basePath.slice(0, -1) : basePath
    11	        return content.replace(
    12	                /(?<![a-zA-Z0-9])@([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+\/[a-zA-Z0-9_.\-\/]*)/g,
    13	                (match, relativePath: string) => {
    14	                        if (!looksLikeFilePath(relativePath)) return match
    15	                        const resolvedPath = resolve(normalizedBase, relativePath)
    16	                        const relativePathFromBase = relative(normalizedBase, resolvedPath)
    17	                        if (relativePathFromBase.startsWith("..") || isAbsolute(relativePathFromBase)) {
    18	                                return match
    19	                        }
    20	                        if (relativePath.endsWith("/") && !resolvedPath.endsWith(sep)) {
    21	                                return `${resolvedPath}/`
    22	                        }
    23	                        return resolvedPath
    24	                }
    25	        )
    26	}
    27

Now I have a good picture. Let me understand the issue better.

The PR describes that skills from the "superpowers" plugin are exposed with short names like `systematic-debugging` but can only be resolved with fully qualified names like `superpowers/systematic-debugging`.

The issue is in how skill names are displayed vs resolved. Let me look at how the `skill` tool resolves names. Going back to `tools.ts`:

1. Skills are discovered with potential `namePrefix` from `skill-directory-loader.ts` (line 74: `const newPrefix = namePrefix ? `${namePrefix}/${dirName}` : dirName`)
2. When showing available items, the full name (with prefix) is shown
3. When looking up, the code does exact match against the full name

Wait, but the PR says the short name is shown. Let me look at the `formatCombinedDescription` more carefully. In `tools.ts` line 106:
```
`    <name>/${skill.name}</name>`,
```

This shows the full name. So if the skill name is `superpowers/systematic-debugging`, it would show `/superpowers/systematic-debugging`. But the PR says `systematic-debugging` is shown.

Let me re-read the PR description: "some superpowers skills are surfaced to the user by their short names (for example systematic-debugging), but the skill resolver does not actually accept those short names."

So maybe the display IS showing the full name, but the user is confused? Or maybe there's a different place where only the short name is shown? Or maybe the issue is that the resolver should also accept short names (the part after the last `/`) as aliases?

Actually, let me re-read: "the error message then suggests using the fully qualified name such as `superpowers/systematic-debugging`". So the skill name stored is `superpowers/systematic-debugging`, and the error suggests using that. But the user says it's "surfaced" as `systematic-debugging` - maybe through the available skills list or somewhere else.

Let me look at how skills are displayed to users in other places. Maybe the issue is in the `availableSkills` list or how the skill context builds the available skills for agents:

    26	export function categorizeTools(toolNames: string[]): AvailableTool[] {
    27	  return toolNames.map((name) => {
    28	    let category: AvailableTool["category"] = "other"
    29	    if (name.startsWith("lsp_")) {
    30	      category = "lsp"
    31	    } else if (name.startsWith("ast_grep")) {
    32	      category = "ast"
    33	    } else if (name === "grep" || name === "glob") {
    34	      category = "search"
    35	    } else if (name.startsWith("session_")) {
    36	      category = "session"
    37	    } else if (name === "skill") {
    38	      category = "command"
    39	    }
    40	    return { name, category }
    41	  })
    42	}
    43	
    44	function formatToolsForPrompt(tools: AvailableTool[]): string {
    45	  const lspTools = tools.filter((t) => t.category === "lsp")
    46	  const astTools = tools.filter((t) => t.category === "ast")
    47	  const searchTools = tools.filter((t) => t.category === "search")
    48	
    49	  const parts: string[] = []
    50	
    51	  if (searchTools.length > 0) {
    52	    parts.push(...searchTools.map((t) => `\`${t.name}\``))
    53	  }
    54	
    55	  if (lspTools.length > 0) {
    56	    parts.push("`lsp_*`")
    57	  }
    58	
    59	  if (astTools.length > 0) {
    60	    parts.push("`ast_grep`")
    61	  }
    62	
    63	  return parts.join(", ")
    64	}

    79	export function buildToolSelectionTable(
    80	  agents: AvailableAgent[],
    81	  tools: AvailableTool[] = [],
    82	  _skills: AvailableSkill[] = []
    83	): string {
    84	  const rows: string[] = [
    85	    "### Tool & Agent Selection:",
    86	    "",
    87	  ]
    88	
    89	  if (tools.length > 0) {
    90	    const toolsDisplay = formatToolsForPrompt(tools)
    91	    rows.push(`- ${toolsDisplay} — **FREE** — Not Complex, Scope Clear, No Implicit Assumptions`)
    92	  }
    93	
    94	  const costOrder = { FREE: 0, CHEAP: 1, EXPENSIVE: 2 }
    95	  const sortedAgents = [...agents]
    96	    .filter((a) => a.metadata.category !== "utility")
    97	    .sort((a, b) => costOrder[a.metadata.cost] - costOrder[b.metadata.cost])
    98	
    99	  for (const agent of sortedAgents) {
   100	    const shortDesc = agent.description.split(".")[0] || agent.description
   101	    rows.push(`- \`${agent.name}\` agent — **${agent.metadata.cost}** — ${shortDesc}`)
   102	  }
   103	
   104	  rows.push("")
   105	  rows.push("**Default flow**: explore/librarian (background) + tools → oracle (if required)")
   106	
   107	  return rows.join("\n")
   108	}

   165

   202	> Full skill descriptions → use the \`skill\` tool to check before EVERY delegation.`

   205	  }

   338	export function buildAntiPatternsSection(): string {
   339	  const patterns = [
   340	    "- **Type Safety**: `as any`, `@ts-ignore`, `@ts-expect-error`",

The key issue is: the `skill` tool's execute function matches by exact name. If a user sees the skill listed somewhere with just the short name (like `systematic-debugging`), they'll try to call `skill(name="systematic-debugging")` and it will fail because the actual stored name is `superpowers/systematic-debugging`.

But looking at the code, the available items in the tool description show the full name with the prefix. So maybe there's a different place where short names are shown. Or maybe the issue is that the resolver should also try to match against just the last part of the name (after `/`).

Actually, I think the fix should be in the `tools.ts` execute function: when looking up a skill, after the exact match fails, try matching against just the last segment of the name (the part after `/`). That way both `superpowers/systematic-debugging` and `systematic-debugging` would work.

import type { LoadedSkill } from "./src/features/opencode-skill-loader/types"

// Simulate skills that come from nested directories (like superpowers/xxx)
const loadedSkills: LoadedSkill[] = [
  {
    name: "superpowers/systematic-debugging",
    path: "/test/skills/superpowers/systematic-debugging/SKILL.md",
    resolvedPath: "/test/skills/superpowers/systematic-debugging",
    definition: {
      name: "superpowers/systematic-debugging",
      description: "Test skill for systematic debugging",
      template: "Test template",
    },
    scope: "opencode",
  },
  {
    name: "superpowers/brainstorming",
    path: "/test/skills/superpowers/brainstorming/SKILL.md",
    resolvedPath: "/test/skills/superpowers/brainstorming",
    definition: {
      name: "superpowers/brainstorming",
      description: "Test skill for brainstorming",
      template: "Test template",
    },
    scope: "opencode",
  },

    resolvedPath: "/test/skills/my-flat-skill",
    definition: {
      name: "my-flat-skill",
      description: "Test flat skill",
      template: "Test template",
    },
    scope: "project",
  },
]

// Test 1: Exact match with full name works
async function testFullName() {
  try {
    const result = await tool.execute({ name: "superpowers/systematic-debugging" })
    console.log("✓ Full name lookup works:", result.substring(0, 50))
  } catch (e) {
    console.log("✗ Full name lookup failed:", e.message)
  }
}

// Test 2: Short name fails
async function testShortName() {
  try {
    const result = await tool.execute({ name: "systematic-debugging" })
    console.log("✓ Short name lookup works:", result.substring(0, 50))
  } catch (e) {
    console.log("✗ Short name lookup failed:", e.message)
  }
}

// Test 3: Partial match in error
async function testNotFound() {
  try {
    await tool.execute({ name: "nonexistent" })
  } catch (e) {
    console.log("Not found error:", e.message)
  }
}

await testFullName()
await testShortName()
await testNotFound()

  console.log(match[1])
}

```typescript
// Check skills first (exact match, case-insensitive)

```

The fix should be: if an exact match fails, try to match just the last segment of the name. But we need to handle potential ambiguities (if two skills have the same short name from different prefixes).

Let me now implement the fix. The approach:
1. First try exact match (as currently done)
2. If no exact match, try matching by the last segment (after `/`) of the skill name
3. If there are multiple matches, it's ambiguous - we should probably still fail but with a better error

      const skills = await getSkills()
      const commands = getCommands()
      cachedDescription = formatCombinedDescription(skills.map(loadedSkillToInfo), commands)

      const requestedName = args.name.replace(/^\//, "")
      const requestedNameLower = requestedName.toLowerCase()

      // Check skills first (exact match, case-insensitive)
      let matchedSkill = skills.find(s => s.name.toLowerCase() === requestedNameLower)

      // If no exact match, try matching by short name (last segment after /)
      if (!matchedSkill) {
        const shortNameMatches = skills.filter(
          s => s.name.includes("/") && s.name.split("/").pop()?.toLowerCase() === requestedNameLower
        )
        if (shortNameMatches.length === 1) {
          matchedSkill = shortNameMatches[0]
        }
      }

      if (matchedSkill) {
        if (matchedSkill.definition.agent && (!ctx?.agent || matchedSkill.definition.agent !== ctx.agent)) {
          throw new Error(`Skill "${matchedSkill.name}" is restricted to agent "${matchedSkill.definition.agent}"`)
        }

        let body = await extractSkillBody(matchedSkill)

        if (matchedSkill.name === "git-master") {
          body = injectGitMasterConfig(body, options.gitMasterConfig)
        }

        const dir = matchedSkill.path ? dirname(matchedSkill.path) : matchedSkill.resolvedPath || process.cwd()

        const output = [
          `## Skill: ${matchedSkill.name}`,
          "",
          `**Base directory**: ${dir}`,
          "",
          body,
        ]

        if (options.mcpManager && options.getSessionID && matchedSkill.mcpConfig) {
          const mcpInfo = await formatMcpCapabilities(
            matchedSkill,
            options.mcpManager,
            options.getSessionID()
          )
          if (mcpInfo) {
            output.push(mcpInfo)
          }
        }

        return output.join("\n")
      }

      // Check commands (exact match, case-insensitive) - sort by priority first
      const sortedCommands = [...commands].sort((a, b) => {
        const priorityA = scopePriority[a.scope] || 0
        const priorityB = scopePriority[b.scope] || 0
        return priorityB - priorityA // Higher priority first
      })
      const matchedCommand = sortedCommands.find(c => c.name.toLowerCase() === requestedNameLower)

      if (matchedCommand) {
        return await formatLoadedCommand(matchedCommand, args.user_message)
      }

      // No match found — provide helpful error with partial matches
      const allNames = [
        ...skills.map(s => s.name),
        ...commands.map(c => `/${c.name}`),
      ]

      const partialMatches = allNames.filter(n =>
        n.toLowerCase().includes(requestedNameLower)
      )

      if (partialMatches.length > 0) {
        throw new Error(
          `Skill or command "${args.name}" not found. Did you mean: ${partialMatches.join(", ")}?`
        )
      }

      const available = allNames.join(", ")
      throw new Error(
        `Skill or command "${args.name}" not found. Available: ${available || "none"}`
      )
    },'

     8	): Promise<{ content: string | undefined; contents: string[]; error: string | null }> {

     1	import { createBuiltinSkills } from "../builtin-skills/skills"
     2	import type { LoadedSkill } from "./types"
     3	import type { SkillResolutionOptions } from "./skill-resolution-options"
     4	import { injectGitMasterConfig } from "./git-master-template-injection"
     5	import { getAllSkills } from "./skill-discovery"
     6	import { extractSkillTemplate } from "./loaded-skill-template-extractor"
     7	
     8	export function resolveSkillContent(skillName: string, options?: SkillResolutionOptions): string | null {
     9	        const skills = createBuiltinSkills({
    10	                browserProvider: options?.browserProvider,
    11	                disabledSkills: options?.disabledSkills,
    12	        })
    13	        const skill = skills.find((builtinSkill) => builtinSkill.name === skillName)
    14	        if (!skill) return null
    15	
    16	        if (skillName === "git-master") {
    17	                return injectGitMasterConfig(skill.template, options?.gitMasterConfig)
    18	        }
    19	
    20	        return skill.template
    21	}
    22	
    23	export function resolveMultipleSkills(
    24	        skillNames: string[],
    25	        options?: SkillResolutionOptions
    26	): { resolved: Map<string, string>; notFound: string[] } {
    27	        const skills = createBuiltinSkills({
    28	                browserProvider: options?.browserProvider,

        name: string,
        allSkills: LoadedSkill[]
): LoadedSkill | undefined {
        const lowerName = name.toLowerCase()
        const shortNameMatches = allSkills.filter(
                s => s.name.includes("/") && s.name.split("/").pop()?.toLowerCase() === lowerName
        )
        // Only use short name match if it'"'"'s unambiguous (exactly one match)
        if (shortNameMatches.length === 1) {
                return shortNameMatches[0]
        }
        return undefined
}

export async function resolveSkillContentAsync(
        skillName: string,
        options?: SkillResolutionOptions
): Promise<string | null> {
        const allSkills = await getAllSkills(options)
        let skill = allSkills.find((loadedSkill) => loadedSkill.name === skillName)
        if (!skill) {
                skill = resolveByShortName(skillName, allSkills)
        }
        if (!skill) return null

        const template = await extractSkillTemplate(skill)

        if (skillName === "git-master") {
                return injectGitMasterConfig(template, options?.gitMasterConfig)
        }

        return template
}

export async function resolveMultipleSkillsAsync(
        skillNames: string[],
        options?: SkillResolutionOptions
): Promise<{ resolved: Map<string, string>; notFound: string[] }> {
        const allSkills = await getAllSkills(options)
        const skillMap = new Map<string, LoadedSkill>()
        for (const skill of allSkills) {
                skillMap.set(skill.name, skill)
        }

        const resolved = new Map<string, string>()
        const notFound: string[] = []

        for (const name of skillNames) {
                let skill = skillMap.get(name)
                if (!skill) {
                        skill = resolveByShortName(name, allSkills)
                }
                if (skill) {
                        const template = await extractSkillTemplate(skill)
                        if (name === "git-master") {
                                resolved.set(name, injectGitMasterConfig(template, options?.gitMasterConfig))
                        } else {
                                resolved.set(name, template)
                        }
                } else {
                        notFound.push(name)
                }
        }

        return { resolved, notFound }

    13	  path?: string
    14	  metadata: CommandMetadata

    22	function skillToCommandInfo(skill: LoadedSkill): SkillCommandInfo {
    23	  return {
    24	    name: skill.name,
    25	    path: skill.path,

    33	    },

    40	export interface ExecutorOptions {
    41	  skills?: LoadedSkill[]
    42	  pluginsEnabled?: boolean
    43	  enabledPluginsOverride?: Record<string, boolean>
    44	  agent?: string
    45	  directory?: string
    46	}
    47	
    48	
    49	async function discoverAllCommands(options?: ExecutorOptions): Promise<CommandInfo[]> {
    50	  const discoveredCommands = discoverCommandsSync(options?.directory ?? process.cwd(), {
    51	    pluginsEnabled: options?.pluginsEnabled,
    52	    enabledPluginsOverride: options?.enabledPluginsOverride,
    53	  })
    54	
    55	  const skills = options?.skills ?? await discoverAllSkills()
    56	  const skillCommands = skills.map(skillToCommandInfo)
    57	
    58	  const scopeOrder: DiscoveredCommandInfo["scope"][] = ["project", "user", "opencode-project", "opencode", "builtin", "plugin"]
    59	  const grouped = new Map<string, DiscoveredCommandInfo[]>()
    60	  for (const cmd of discoveredCommands) {
    61	    const list = grouped.get(cmd.scope) ?? []
    62	    list.push(cmd)
    63	    grouped.set(cmd.scope, list)
    64	  }
    65	  const orderedCommands = scopeOrder.flatMap((scope) => grouped.get(scope) ?? [])
    66	
    67	  return [
    68	    ...skillCommands,
    69	    ...orderedCommands,
    70	  ]
    71	}
    72	
    73	async function findCommand(commandName: string, options?: ExecutorOptions): Promise<CommandInfo | null> {
    74	  const allCommands = await discoverAllCommands(options)
    75	  return allCommands.find(
    76	    (cmd) => cmd.name.toLowerCase() === commandName.toLowerCase()
    77	  ) ?? null
    78	}
    79	
    80	async function formatCommandTemplate(cmd: CommandInfo, args: string): Promise<string> {
    81	  const sections: string[] = []
    82	
    83	  sections.push(`# /${cmd.name} Command\n`)
    84	
    85	  if (cmd.metadata.description) {
    86	    sections.push(`**Description**: ${cmd.metadata.description}\n`)
    87	  }
    88	
    89	  if (args) {
    90	    sections.push(`**User Arguments**: ${args}\n`)
    91	  }
    92	
    93	  if (cmd.metadata.model) {
    94	    sections.push(`**Model**: ${cmd.metadata.model}\n`)
    95	  }
    96	
    97	  if (cmd.metadata.agent) {
    98	    sections.push(`**Agent**: ${cmd.metadata.agent}\n`)
    99	  }
   100	
   101	  sections.push(`**Scope**: ${cmd.scope}\n`)
   102	  sections.push("---\n")
   103	  sections.push("## Command Instructions\n")
   104	
   105	  let content = cmd.content || ""
   106	  if (!content && cmd.lazyContentLoader) {
   107	    content = await cmd.lazyContentLoader.load()
   108	  }
   109	
   110	  const commandDir = cmd.path ? dirname(cmd.path) : process.cwd()
   111	  const withFileRefs = await resolveFileReferencesInText(content, commandDir)
   112	  const resolvedContent = await resolveCommandsInText(withFileRefs)
   113	  const resolvedArguments = args
   114	  const substitutedContent = resolvedContent
   115	    .replace(/\$\{user_message\}/g, resolvedArguments)
   116	    .replace(/\$ARGUMENTS/g, resolvedArguments)
   117	  sections.push(substitutedContent.trim())
   118	
   119	  if (args) {
   120	    sections.push("\n\n---\n")
   121	    sections.push("## User Request\n")
   122	    sections.push(args)
   123	  }
   124	
   125	  return sections.join("\n")
   126	}
   127	
   128	export interface ExecuteResult {
   129	  success: boolean
   130	  replacementText?: string
   131	  error?: string
   132	}
   133	
   134	export async function executeSlashCommand(parsed: ParsedSlashCommand, options?: ExecutorOptions): Promise<ExecuteResult> {
   135	  const command = await findCommand(parsed.command, options)
   136	
   137	  if (!command) {
   138	    return {
   139	      success: false,
   140	      error: `Command "/${parsed.command}" not found. Use the skill tool to list available skills and commands.`,
   141	    }
   142	  }
   143	
   144	  if (command.scope === "skill" && command.metadata.agent) {
   145	    if (!options?.agent || command.metadata.agent !== options.agent) {
   146	      return {
   147	        success: false,
   148	        error: `Skill "${command.name}" is restricted to agent "${command.metadata.agent}"`,
   149	      }
   150	    }
   151	  }
   152	
   153	  try {
   154	    const template = await formatCommandTemplate(command, parsed.args)
   155	    return {
   156	      success: true,
   157	      replacementText: template,
   158	    }
   159	  } catch (err) {
   160	    return {
   161	      success: false,
   162	      error: `Failed to load command "/${parsed.command}": ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}`,
   163	    }
   164	  }
   165	}

     1	import {
     2	  detectSlashCommand,
     3	  extractPromptText,
     4	  findSlashCommandPartIndex,
     5	} from "./detector"
     6	import { executeSlashCommand, type ExecutorOptions } from "./executor"
     7	import { log } from "../../shared"
     8	import {
     9	  AUTO_SLASH_COMMAND_TAG_CLOSE,
    10	  AUTO_SLASH_COMMAND_TAG_OPEN,
    11	} from "./constants"
    12	import { createProcessedCommandStore } from "./processed-command-store"
    13	import type {
    14	  AutoSlashCommandHookInput,
    15	  AutoSlashCommandHookOutput,
    16	  CommandExecuteBeforeInput,
    17	  CommandExecuteBeforeOutput,
    18	} from "./types"
    19	import type { LoadedSkill } from "../../features/opencode-skill-loader"
    20	
    21	const COMMAND_EXECUTE_FALLBACK_DEDUP_TTL_MS = 100
    22	
    23	function isRecord(value: unknown): value is Record<string, unknown> {
    24	  return typeof value === "object" && value !== null
    25	}
    26	
    27	function getDeletedSessionID(properties: unknown): string | null {
    28	  if (!isRecord(properties)) {
    29	    return null
    30	  }
    31	
    32	  const info = properties.info
    33	  if (!isRecord(info)) {
    34	    return null
    35	  }
    36	
    37	  return typeof info.id === "string" ? info.id : null
    38	}
    39	
    40	function getCommandExecutionEventID(input: CommandExecuteBeforeInput): string | null {
    41	  const candidateKeys = [
    42	    "messageID",
    43	    "messageId",
    44	    "eventID",
    45	    "eventId",
    46	    "invocationID",
    47	    "invocationId",
    48	    "commandID",
    49	    "commandId",
    50	  ]
    51	
    52	  const recordInput = input as unknown
    53	  if (!isRecord(recordInput)) {
    54	    return null
    55	  }
    56	
    57	  for (const key of candidateKeys) {
    58	    const candidateValue = recordInput[key]
    59	    if (typeof candidateValue === "string" && candidateValue.length > 0) {
    60	      return candidateValue
    61	    }
    62	  }
    63	
    64	  return null
    65	}
    66	
    67	export interface AutoSlashCommandHookOptions {
    68	  skills?: LoadedSkill[]
    69	  pluginsEnabled?: boolean
    70	  enabledPluginsOverride?: Record<string, boolean>
    71	  directory?: string
    72	}
    73	
    74	export function createAutoSlashCommandHook(options?: AutoSlashCommandHookOptions) {
    75	  const executorOptions: ExecutorOptions = {
    76	    skills: options?.skills,
    77	    pluginsEnabled: options?.pluginsEnabled,
    78	    enabledPluginsOverride: options?.enabledPluginsOverride,
    79	    directory: options?.directory,
    80	  }
    81	  const sessionProcessedCommands = createProcessedCommandStore()
    82	  const sessionProcessedCommandExecutions = createProcessedCommandStore()
    83	
    84	  const dispose = (): void => {
    85	    sessionProcessedCommands.clear()
    86	    sessionProcessedCommandExecutions.clear()
    87	  }
    88	
    89	  return {
    90	    "chat.message": async (
    91	      input: AutoSlashCommandHookInput,
    92	      output: AutoSlashCommandHookOutput
    93	    ): Promise<void> => {
    94	      const promptText = extractPromptText(output.parts)
    95	
    96	      // Debug logging to diagnose slash command issues
    97	      if (promptText.startsWith("/")) {
    98	        log(`[auto-slash-command] chat.message hook received slash command`, {
    99	          sessionID: input.sessionID,
   100	          promptText: promptText.slice(0, 100),
   101	        })
   102	      }
   103	
   104	      if (
   105	        promptText.includes(AUTO_SLASH_COMMAND_TAG_OPEN) ||
   106	        promptText.includes(AUTO_SLASH_COMMAND_TAG_CLOSE)
   107	      ) {
   108	        return
   109	      }
   110	
   111	      const parsed = detectSlashCommand(promptText)
   112	
   113	      if (!parsed) {
   114	        return
   115	      }
   116	
   117	      const commandKey = input.messageID
   118	        ? `${input.sessionID}:${input.messageID}:${parsed.command}`
   119	        : `${input.sessionID}:${parsed.command}`
   120	      if (sessionProcessedCommands.has(commandKey)) {
   121	        return
   122	      }
   123	      sessionProcessedCommands.add(commandKey)
   124	
   125	      log(`[auto-slash-command] Detected: /${parsed.command}`, {
   126	        sessionID: input.sessionID,
   127	        args: parsed.args,
   128	      })
   129	
   130	      const executionOptions: ExecutorOptions = {
   131	        ...executorOptions,
   132	        agent: input.agent,
   133	      }
   134	
   135	      const result = await executeSlashCommand(parsed, executionOptions)
   136	
   137	      const idx = findSlashCommandPartIndex(output.parts)
   138	      if (idx < 0) {
   139	        return
   140	      }
   141	
   142	      if (!result.success || !result.replacementText) {
   143	        log(`[auto-slash-command] Command not found, skipping`, {
   144	          sessionID: input.sessionID,
   145	          command: parsed.command,
   146	          error: result.error,
   147	        })
   148	        return
   149	      }
   150	
   151	      const taggedContent = `${AUTO_SLASH_COMMAND_TAG_OPEN}\n${result.replacementText}\n${AUTO_SLASH_COMMAND_TAG_CLOSE}`
   152	      output.parts[idx].text = taggedContent
   153	
   154	      log(`[auto-slash-command] Replaced message with command template`, {
   155	        sessionID: input.sessionID,
   156	        command: parsed.command,
   157	      })
   158	    },
   159	
   160	    "command.execute.before": async (
   161	      input: CommandExecuteBeforeInput,
   162	      output: CommandExecuteBeforeOutput
   163	    ): Promise<void> => {
   164	      const eventID = getCommandExecutionEventID(input)
   165	      const commandKey = eventID
   166	        ? `${input.sessionID}:event:${eventID}`
   167	        : `${input.sessionID}:fallback:${input.command.toLowerCase()}:${input.arguments || ""}`
   168	      if (sessionProcessedCommandExecutions.has(commandKey)) {
   169	        return
   170	      }
   171	
   172	      log(`[auto-slash-command] command.execute.before received`, {
   173	        sessionID: input.sessionID,
   174	        command: input.command,
   175	        arguments: input.arguments,
   176	      })
   177	
   178	      const parsed = {
   179	        command: input.command,
   180	        args: input.arguments || "",
   181	        raw: `/${input.command}${input.arguments ? " " + input.arguments : ""}`,
   182	      }
   183	
   184	      const executionOptions: ExecutorOptions = {
   185	        ...executorOptions,
   186	        agent: input.agent,
   187	      }
   188	
   189	      const result = await executeSlashCommand(parsed, executionOptions)
   190	
   191	      if (!result.success || !result.replacementText) {
   192	        log(`[auto-slash-command] command.execute.before - command not found in our executor`, {
   193	          sessionID: input.sessionID,
   194	          command: input.command,
   195	          error: result.error,
   196	        })
   197	        return
   198	      }
   199	
   200	      sessionProcessedCommandExecutions.add(
   201	        commandKey,
   202	        eventID ? undefined : COMMAND_EXECUTE_FALLBACK_DEDUP_TTL_MS
   203	      )
   204	
   205	      const taggedContent = `${AUTO_SLASH_COMMAND_TAG_OPEN}\n${result.replacementText}\n${AUTO_SLASH_COMMAND_TAG_CLOSE}`
   206	
   207	      const idx = findSlashCommandPartIndex(output.parts)
   208	      if (idx >= 0) {
   209	        output.parts[idx].text = taggedContent
   210	      } else {
   211	        output.parts.unshift({ type: "text", text: taggedContent })
   212	      }
   213	
   214	      log(`[auto-slash-command] command.execute.before - injected template`, {
   215	        sessionID: input.sessionID,
   216	        command: input.command,
   217	      })
   218	    },
   219	    event: async ({
   220	      event,
   221	    }: {
   222	      event: { type: string; properties?: unknown }
   223	    }): Promise<void> => {
   224	      if (event.type !== "session.deleted") {
   225	        return
   226	      }
   227	
   228	      const sessionID = getDeletedSessionID(event.properties)
   229	      if (!sessionID) {
   230	        return
   231	      }
   232	
   233	      sessionProcessedCommands.cleanupSession(sessionID)
   234	      sessionProcessedCommandExecutions.cleanupSession(sessionID)
   235	    },
   236	    dispose,
   237	  }
   238	}
   239

But `/nonexistent-command` should not match any of those. Unless... wait, the issue is the `<auto-slash-command>` tags wrapping the original text. Let me look at the hook code again:

Line 142-148:
```typescript
if (!result.success || !result.replacementText) {
    log(...)
    return
}
```

If `result.success` is true AND `result.replacementText` is truthy, it proceeds to wrap in tags. If `result.success` is false, it returns without modifying.

So the question is: why is `executeSlashCommand` returning `{ success: true, replacementText: "/nonexistent-command args" }` for an unknown command?

Wait, let me re-read the error output more carefully:

```
- "/nonexistent-command args"
+ "<auto-slash-command>
+ /nonexistent-command args
+ </auto-slash-command>"
```

The replacement text is just `/nonexistent-command args` - the original slash command text. This suggests `executeSlashCommand` is finding a match somehow and returning a template that just echoes back the command text.

But looking at `formatCommandTemplate`, it builds a more complex output: `"# /{cmd.name} Command\n\n**Description**: ..."`. It wouldn't just return the raw command.

Unless... the `findCommand` function is matching something. Let me check: with my short-name fix, if there's a skill whose name ends with `nonexistent-command`, it would match. But that seems unlikely.

-  return allCommands.find(

+  const lowerName = commandName.toLowerCase()
+  const exactMatch = allCommands.find(
+    (cmd) => cmd.name.toLowerCase() === lowerName
+  )
+  if (exactMatch) return exactMatch
+
+  // Fallback to short name matching (last segment after /)
+  const shortNameMatches = allCommands.filter(
+    (cmd) => cmd.name.includes("/") && cmd.name.split("/").pop()?.toLowerCase() === lowerName
+  )
+  if (shortNameMatches.length === 1) {
+    return shortNameMatches[0]
+  }
+  return null
