import { createSkillTool } from "./src/tools/skill/tools"
import type { LoadedSkill } from "./src/features/opencode-skill-loader/types"

// Simulate skills from nested directories
const loadedSkills: LoadedSkill[] = [
  {
    name: "superpowers/systematic-debugging",
    path: undefined,
    resolvedPath: "/test/skills/superpowers/systematic-debugging",
    definition: {
      name: "superpowers/systematic-debugging",
      description: "Test skill for systematic debugging",
      template: "<skill-instruction>\nDebug systematically.\n</skill-instruction>",
    },
    scope: "opencode",
  },
  {
    name: "superpowers/brainstorming",
    path: undefined,
    resolvedPath: "/test/skills/superpowers/brainstorming",
    definition: {
      name: "superpowers/brainstorming",
      description: "Test skill for brainstorming",
      template: "<skill-instruction>\nBrainstorm ideas.\n</skill-instruction>",
    },
    scope: "opencode",
  },
  {
    name: "my-flat-skill",
    path: undefined,
    resolvedPath: "/test/skills/my-flat-skill",
    definition: {
      name: "my-flat-skill",
      description: "Test flat skill",
      template: "<skill-instruction>\nFlat skill body.\n</skill-instruction>",
    },
    scope: "project",
  },
]

const tool = createSkillTool({ skills: loadedSkills })

async function runTests() {
  // Test 1: Exact match with full name
  try {
    const result = await tool.execute({ name: "superpowers/systematic-debugging" })
    console.log("✓ Full name lookup works:", result.includes("superpowers/systematic-debugging"))
  } catch (e: any) {
    console.log("✗ Full name lookup failed:", e.message)
  }

  // Test 2: Short name should now work
  try {
    const result = await tool.execute({ name: "systematic-debugging" })
    console.log("✓ Short name lookup works:", result.includes("superpowers/systematic-debugging"))
  } catch (e: any) {
    console.log("✗ Short name lookup failed:", e.message)
  }

  // Test 3: Short name for other nested skill
  try {
    const result = await tool.execute({ name: "brainstorming" })
    console.log("✓ Short name for brainstorming works:", result.includes("superpowers/brainstorming"))
  } catch (e: any) {
    console.log("✗ Short name for brainstorming failed:", e.message)
  }

  // Test 4: Flat skill still works
  try {
    const result = await tool.execute({ name: "my-flat-skill" })
    console.log("✓ Flat skill works:", result.includes("my-flat-skill"))
  } catch (e: any) {
    console.log("✗ Flat skill failed:", e.message)
  }

  // Test 5: Ambiguous short name (two skills with same short name from different prefixes)
  const skillsWithDuplicate: LoadedSkill[] = [
    {
      name: "superpowers/brainstorming",
      path: undefined,
      resolvedPath: "/test/skills/superpowers/brainstorming",
      definition: {
        name: "superpowers/brainstorming",
        description: "Superpowers brainstorming",
        template: "<skill-instruction>\nBrainstorm ideas from superpowers.\n</skill-instruction>",
      },
      scope: "opencode",
    },
    {
      name: "other/brainstorming",
      path: undefined,
      resolvedPath: "/test/skills/other/brainstorming",
      definition: {
        name: "other/brainstorming",
        description: "Other brainstorming",
        template: "<skill-instruction>\nBrainstorm ideas from other.\n</skill-instruction>",
      },
      scope: "user",
    },
  ]
  const tool2 = createSkillTool({ skills: skillsWithDuplicate })

  try {
    const result = await tool2.execute({ name: "brainstorming" })
    console.log("✗ Ambiguous short name should not resolve:", result.substring(0, 100))
  } catch (e: any) {
    console.log("✓ Ambiguous short name correctly fails:", e.message.includes("Did you mean"))
  }

  // Test 6: Non-existent short name
  try {
    await tool.execute({ name: "nonexistent" })
  } catch (e: any) {
    console.log("✓ Non-existent short name correctly fails:", e.message.includes("not found"))
  }

  // Test 7: Case insensitivity for short names
  try {
    const result = await tool.execute({ name: "SYSTEMATIC-DEBUGGING" })
    console.log("✓ Case-insensitive short name works:", result.includes("superpowers/systematic-debugging"))
  } catch (e: any) {
    console.log("✗ Case-insensitive short name failed:", e.message)
  }
}

await runTests()

2026-05-30 17:05:19,922 - INFO - swea-agent-code-yeongyu__oh-my-openagent-3013 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now let me also think about edge cases I might have missed:

1. **Skills with no `/` in the name**: Already handled - the short name fallback only activates for skills that have `/` in their name (line: `s.name.includes("/")`). Flat skills like `playwright` are matched by exact name.

2. **Skills with multiple `/`**: e.g., `a/b/c/skill`. The `split("/").pop()` gives `skill`, which is the right short name.

3. **What if a short name matches a flat skill exactly?**: The exact match is tried first, so `playwright` would match the flat `playwright` skill before trying short name fallback.

4. **What about commands?**: Commands don't have the nested directory naming - they use flat names or `plugin:command` format. The `pluginsEnabled` path handles those separately. The short name fallback in `tools.ts` only applies to skills, not commands. In `executor.ts`, it applies to all commands (including skill-commands).

5. **What about the `resolveMultipleSkills` (sync) function?**: It uses `createBuiltinSkills` which returns skills with flat names only (no prefixes). So it doesn't need the short name fix.

Now let me verify all the files I've changed:

+function resolveByShortName(
+        name: string,
+        allSkills: LoadedSkill[]
+): LoadedSkill | undefined {
+        const lowerName = name.toLowerCase()
+        const shortNameMatches = allSkills.filter(

+        const notFound: string[] = []

+                        }

+                }
+        }

+function resolveByShortName(
+        name: string,
+        allSkills: LoadedSkill[]
+): LoadedSkill | undefined {
+        const lowerName = name.toLowerCase()
+        const shortNameMatches = allSkills.filter(
+                s => s.name.includes("/") && s.name.split("/").pop()?.toLowerCase() === lowerName
+        )
+        // Only use short name match if it's unambiguous (exactly one match)
+        if (shortNameMatches.length === 1) {
+                return shortNameMatches[0]
+        }
+        return undefined
